<h5><a id="user-content-documentation-workflow-map" class="anchor" href="#documentation-workflow-map" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Documentation Workflow Map</h5>

<h2></h2>

<h4><a id="user-content-table-of-contents" class="anchor" href="#table-of-contents" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Table of Contents</h4>

<h2><a id="user-content-overview" class="anchor" href="#overview" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Overview</h2>

<p>The ciscopuppet module allows a network administrator to manage Cisco Network Elements using Puppet. This module bundles a set of Puppet Types, providers, Beaker Tests, Sample Manifests and Installation Tools for effective network management.  The  resources and capabilities provided by this Puppet Module will grow with contributions from Cisco, Puppet Labs and the open source community.</p>

<p>The Cisco Network Elements and Operating Systems managed by this Puppet Module are continuously expanding. Please refer to the <a href="#limitations">Limitations</a> section for details on currently supported hardware and software.
The Limitations section also provides details on compatible Puppet Agent and Puppet Master versions.</p>

<p>This GitHub repository contains the latest version of the ciscopuppet module source code. Supported versions of the ciscopuppet module are available at Puppet Forge. Please refer to <a href="/cisco/cisco-network-puppet-module/blob/develop/SUPPORT.md">SUPPORT.md</a> for additional details.</p>

<p>Contributions to this Puppet Module are welcome. Guidelines on contributions to the module are captured in <a href="/cisco/cisco-network-puppet-module/blob/develop/CONTRIBUTING.md">CONTRIBUTING.md</a></p>

<h2><a id="user-content-module-description" class="anchor" href="#module-description" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Module Description</h2>

<p>This module enables management of supported Cisco Network Elements using Puppet. This module enhances the Puppet DSL by introducing new Puppet Types and Providers capable of managing network elements.</p>

<p>The set of supported network element platforms is continuously expanding. Please refer to the <a href="#limitations">Limitations</a> section for a list of currently supported platforms.</p>

<h2><a id="user-content-setup" class="anchor" href="#setup" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Setup</h2>

<h4><a id="user-content-puppet-master" class="anchor" href="#puppet-master" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Puppet Master</h4>

<p>The <code>ciscopuppet</code> module is installed on the Puppet Master server. Please see <a href="https://docs.puppetlabs.com/puppet/latest/reference/modules_installing.html">Puppet Labs: Installing Modules</a> for general information on Puppet module installation.</p>

<h4><a id="user-content-puppet-agent" class="anchor" href="#puppet-agent" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Puppet Agent</h4>

<p>The Puppet Agent requires installation and setup on each device. Agent setup can be performed as a manual process or it may be automated. For more information please see the <a href="/cisco/cisco-network-puppet-module/blob/develop/docs/README-agent-install.md">README-agent-install.md</a> document for detailed instructions on agent installation and configuration on Cisco Nexus devices.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-artifacts" class="anchor" href="#artifacts" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Artifacts</h5>

<p>As noted in the agent installation guide, these are the current RPM versions for use with ciscopuppet:</p>

<ul>
<li><code>bash-shell</code>: Use <a href="http://yum.puppetlabs.com/puppetlabs-release-pc1-cisco-wrlinux-5.noarch.rpm">http://yum.puppetlabs.com/puppetlabs-release-pc1-cisco-wrlinux-5.noarch.rpm</a></li>
<li><code>guestshell</code>: Use <a href="http://yum.puppetlabs.com/puppetlabs-release-pc1-el-7.noarch.rpm">http://yum.puppetlabs.com/puppetlabs-release-pc1-el-7.noarch.rpm</a></li>
</ul>

<h5><a id="user-content-gems" class="anchor" href="#gems" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Gems</h5>

<p>The ciscopuppet module has dependencies on a few ruby gems. After installing the Puppet Agent software you will then need to install the following gems on the agent device:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="https://rubygems.org/gems/net_http_unix"><code>net_http_unix</code></a></li>
<li><a href="https://rubygems.org/gems/cisco_nxapi"><code>cisco_nxapi</code></a></li>
<li><a href="https://rubygems.org/gems/cisco_node_utils"><code>cisco_node_utils</code></a></li>
</ul>

<p>These gems have dependencies on each other so installing <code>cisco_node_utils</code> by itself will automatically install <code>net_http_unix</code> and <code>cisco_nxapi</code>.</p>

<p>Example:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>[root@guestshell]#  gem install cisco_node_utils

[root@guestshell]#  gem list <span class="pl-k">|</span> egrep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>cisco|net_http<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
cisco_node_utils (1.0.0)
cisco_nxapi (1.0.0)
net_http_unix (0.2.1)</pre></div>

<p><em>Please note: The <code>ciscopuppet</code> module requires a compatible <code>cisco_node_utils</code> gem. This is not an issue with release versions; however, when using a pre-release module it may be necessary to manually build a compatible gem. Please see the <code>cisco_node_utils</code> developer's guide for more information on building a <code>cisco_node_utils</code> gem:  <a href="https://github.com/cisco/cisco-network-node-utils/blob/develop/docs/README-develop-node-utils-APIs.md#step-5-build-and-install-the-gem">README-develop-node-utils-APIs.md</a></em></p>

<h5><a id="user-content-gem-persistence-bash-shell-only" class="anchor" href="#gem-persistence-bash-shell-only" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Gem Persistence (bash-shell only)</h5>

<p>Please note that in the Nexus <code>bash-shell</code> environment these gems are currently not persistent across system reload. This persistence issue can be mitigated by simply defining a manifest entry for installing the <code>cisco_node_utils</code> gem via the package provider.</p>

<p>Example:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-puppet"><pre>package { <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>cisco_node_utils<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> :
  <span class="pl-c1">provider</span> =&gt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>gem<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
  <span class="pl-c1">ensure</span> =&gt; present,
}</pre></div>

<p><em>This persistence issue does not affect the <code>guestshell</code> environment. Gems are persistent across reload in the <code>guestshell</code>.</em></p>

<h2><a id="user-content-usage" class="anchor" href="#usage" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Usage</h2>

<p>The following example shows how to use ciscopuppet to configure ospf on a
Cisco Nexus switch.</p>

<p>Three types are needed to add OSPF support on an interface: cisco_ospf,
cisco_ospf_vrf, and cisco_interface_ospf.</p>

<p>First, to configure cisco_ospf to enable ospf on the device, add the
following type in the manifest:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-puppet"><pre><span class="pl-k">cisco_ospf</span> {<span class="pl-en">"Sample"</span>:
   <span class="pl-c1">ensure</span> =&gt; present,
}</pre></div>

<p>Then put the ospf router under a VRF, and add the corresponding OSPF configuration.
If the configuration is global, use 'default' as the VRF name.</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-puppet"><pre><span class="pl-k">cisco_ospf_vrf</span> {<span class="pl-en">"Sample default"</span>:
   <span class="pl-c1">ensure</span> =&gt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>present<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
   <span class="pl-c1">default_metric</span> =&gt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>5<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
   <span class="pl-c1">auto_cost</span> =&gt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>46000<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,
}</pre></div>

<p>Finally apply the ospf into an interface:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-puppet"><pre><span class="pl-k">cisco_interface_ospf</span> {<span class="pl-en">"Ethernet1/2 Sample"</span>:
   <span class="pl-c1">ensure</span> =&gt; present,
   <span class="pl-c1">area</span> =&gt; 200,
   <span class="pl-c1">cost</span> =&gt; <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>200<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,
}</pre></div>

<h2><a id="user-content-resource-reference" class="anchor" href="#resource-reference" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><a name="user-content-resource-reference">Resource Reference</a></h2>

<p>The following resources include cisco types and providers along with cisco provider support for netdev stdlib types.  Installing the <code>ciscopuppet</code> module will install both the <code>ciscopuppet</code> and <code>netdev_stdlib</code> modules.</p>

<h3><a id="user-content-netdev-stdlib-resource-type-catalog-by-name" class="anchor" href="#netdev-stdlib-resource-type-catalog-by-name" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><a name="user-content-resource-by-name-netdev">NetDev StdLib Resource Type Catalog (by Name)</a></h3>

<ul>

<h2></h2>

<h3><a id="user-content-cisco-resource-type-details" class="anchor" href="#cisco-resource-type-details" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Cisco Resource Type Details</h3>

<h2></h2>

<h3><a id="user-content-type-cisco_command_config" class="anchor" href="#type-cisco_command_config" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Type: cisco_command_config</h3>

<p>Allows execution of configuration commands.</p>

<h4><a id="user-content-parameters" class="anchor" href="#parameters" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Parameters</h4>

<h5><a id="user-content-command" class="anchor" href="#command" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>command</code></h5>

<p>Configuration command(s) to be applied to the network element. Valid values
are string.</p>

<p>This provider allows raw configurations to be managed by Puppet. It serves as a stopgap until specialized types are created. It has the following limitations:</p>

<ul>
<li>The input message buffer is limited to 500KB. Large configurations are often easier to debug if broken up into multiple smaller resource blocks.</li>
<li>The cisco_command_config configuration block must use the same syntax as displayed by the <code>show running-config</code> command on the switch. In some cases, configuration commands that omit optional keywords when entered may actually appear with a different syntax when displayed by <code>show running-config</code>; for example, some access-list entries may be configured without a sequence number but yet an implicit sequence number is created regardless. This then creates an idempotency problem because there is a mismatch between <code>show running-config</code> and the manifest. The solution in this case is for the manifest to include explicit sequence numbers for the affected access-list entries.</li>
<li>Order is important. Some dependent commands may fail if their associated <code>feature</code> configuration is not enabled first. Use Puppet's <code>before</code>, <code>after</code>, or <code>require</code> keywords to establish dependencies between blocks.</li>
<li>Indentation counts! It implies sub-mode configuration. Use the switch's running-config as a guide and do not indent configurations that are not normally indented. Do not use tabs to indent.</li>
<li>Inline comments must be prefixed by '!' or '#'.</li>
<li>Negating a submode will also remove configuratons under that submode, without having to specify every submode config statement: <code>no router ospf RED</code> removes all configuration under router ospf RED.</li>
<li>Syntax does not auto-complete: use <code>Ethernet1/1</code>, not <code>Eth1/1</code>.</li>
<li>If a CLI command is rejected during configuration, the resource will abort at that point and will not issue any remaining CLI. For this reason, we recommend limiting the scope of each instance of this resource.</li>
</ul>

<h2></h2>

<h3><a id="user-content-type-cisco_bgp" class="anchor" href="#type-cisco_bgp" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Type: cisco_bgp</h3>

<p>Manages configuration of a BGP instance.</p>

<h4><a id="user-content-parameters-6" class="anchor" href="#parameters-6" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Parameters</h4>

<h5><a id="user-content-ensure-4" class="anchor" href="#ensure-4" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ensure</code></h5>

<p>Determines whether the config should be present or not on the device. Valid values are 'present' and 'absent'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-asn" class="anchor" href="#asn" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>asn</code></h5>

<p>BGP autonomous system number.  Valid values are String, Integer in ASPLAIN or ASDOT notation.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-vrf" class="anchor" href="#vrf" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>vrf</code></h5>

<p>Name of the resource instance. Valid values are string. The name 'default' is a valid VRF representing the global bgp.</p>

<p><a name="user-content-bgp_rd"></a></p>

<h5><a id="user-content-route_distinguisher" class="anchor" href="#route_distinguisher" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>route_distinguisher</code></h5>

<p>VPN Route Distinguisher (RD). The RD is combined with the IPv4 or IPv6 prefix learned by the PE router to create a globally unique address. Valid values are a String in one of the route-distinguisher formats (ASN2:NN, ASN4:NN, or IPV4:NN); the keyword 'auto', or the keyword 'default'.</p>

<p><em>Please note:</em> The <code>route_distinguisher</code> property is typically configured within the VRF context configuration on most platforms (including NXOS) but it is tightly coupled to bgp and therefore configured within the BGP configuration on some platforms (XR for example). For this reason the <code>route_distinguisher</code> property has support (with limitations) in both <code>cisco_vrf</code> and <code>cisco_bgp</code> providers:</p>

<ul>
<li><code>cisco_bgp</code>: The property is fully supported on both NXOS and XR.</li>
<li><code>cisco_vrf</code>: The property is only supported on NXOS. See: <a href="#vrf_rd">cisco_vrf: route_distinguisher</a></li>
</ul>

<p><em>IMPORTANT: Choose only one provider to configure the <code>route_distinguisher</code> property on a given device. Using both providers simultaneously on the same device may have unpredictable results.</em></p>

<h5><a id="user-content-router_id" class="anchor" href="#router_id" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>router_id</code></h5>

<p>Router Identifier (ID) of the BGP router VRF instance. Valid values are string, and keyword 'default'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-cluster_id" class="anchor" href="#cluster_id" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>cluster_id</code></h5>

<h5><a id="user-content-confederation_peers" class="anchor" href="#confederation_peers" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>confederation_peers</code></h5>

<h5><a id="user-content-disable_policy_batching" class="anchor" href="#disable_policy_batching" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>disable_policy_batching</code></h5>

<p>Enable/Disable deterministic selection of the best MED path from among the paths from the same autonomous system. Valid values are 'true', 'false', and 'default'</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-inject_map" class="anchor" href="#inject_map" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>inject_map</code></h5>

<p>An array of route-map names which will specify prefixes to inject. Each array entry must first specify the inject-map name, secondly an exist-map name, and optionally the <code>copy-attributes</code> keyword which indicates that attributes should be copied from the aggregate.</p>

<p>For example, the following array will create three separate inject-maps for <code>lax_inject_map</code>, <code>nyc_inject_map</code> (with copy-attributes), and <code>fsd_exist_map</code>:</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-ruby"><pre>[
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lax_inject_map<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lax_exist_map<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>nyc_inject_map<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>nyc_exist_map<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>copy-attributes<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>fsd_inject_map<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>fsd_exist_map<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>]
]</pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-maximum_paths" class="anchor" href="#maximum_paths" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>maximum_paths</code></h5>

<p>Configures the maximum number of equal-cost paths for load sharing. Valid value is an integer in the range 1-64. Default value is 1.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-maximum_paths_ibgp" class="anchor" href="#maximum_paths_ibgp" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>maximum_paths_ibgp</code></h5>

<p>Configures the maximum number of ibgp equal-cost paths for load sharing. Valid value is an integer in the range 1-64. Default value is 1.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-networks" class="anchor" href="#networks" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>networks</code></h5>

<p>Networks to configure. Valid value is a list of network prefixes to advertise.  The list must be in the form of an array.  Each entry in the array must include a prefix address and an optional route-map.</p>

<p>Example: IPv4 Networks Array</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-ruby"><pre>[
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>10.0.0.0/16<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>routemap_LA<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>192.168.1.1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Chicago<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>192.168.2.0/24],</span>
<span class="pl-s"> [<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-c1">192.168</span>.<span class="pl-c1">3.0</span><span class="pl-k">/</span><span class="pl-c1">24</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>, <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>routemap_NYC<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>]</span>
<span class="pl-s">]</span></pre></div>

<p>Example: IPv6 Networks Array</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-ruby"><pre>[
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>10::0/64<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>routemap_LA<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>192:168::1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Chicago<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>192:168::/32]</span>
<span class="pl-s">]</span></pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-next_hop_route_map" class="anchor" href="#next_hop_route_map" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>next_hop_route_map</code></h5>

<p>Configure route map for valid nexthops. Valid values are a string defining the name of the route-map.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-redistribute" class="anchor" href="#redistribute" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>redistribute</code></h5>

<p>A list of redistribute directives. Multiple redistribute entries are allowed. The list must be in the form of a nested array: the first entry of each array defines the source-protocol to redistribute from; the second entry defines a route-map/route-policy name. A route-map/route-policy is highly advised but may be optional on some platforms, in which case it may be omitted from the array list.</p>

<p>Example: Platform requiring route-maps</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-ruby"><pre>redistribute =&gt; [[<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>direct<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_direct<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lisp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_lisp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>static<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_static<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>eigrp 1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_eigrp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>isis 2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_isis<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>ospf 3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_ospf<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rip 4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,   <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_rip<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>]]</pre></div>

<p>Example: Platform with optional route-maps</p>

<div class="highlight highlight-source-ruby"><pre>redistribute =&gt; [[<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>direct<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>lisp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_lisp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>static<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>eigrp 1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>, <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_eigrp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>isis 2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_isis<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>ospf 3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>,  <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm_ospf<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>],
                 [<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rip 4<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>]]</pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-suppress_inactive" class="anchor" href="#suppress_inactive" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>suppress_inactive</code></h5>

<p>Advertises only active routes to peersy. Valid values are true, false, or 'default'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-table_map" class="anchor" href="#table_map" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>table_map</code></h5>

<p>Apply table-map to filter routes downloaded into URIB. Valid values are a string.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-table_map_filter" class="anchor" href="#table_map_filter" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>table_map_filter</code></h5>

<p>Filters routes rejected by the route map and does not download them to the RIB. Valid values are true, false, or 'default'.</p>

<h2></h2>

<h3><a id="user-content-type-cisco_bgp_neighbor" class="anchor" href="#type-cisco_bgp_neighbor" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Type: cisco_bgp_neighbor</h3>

<p>Manages configuration of a BGP Neighbor.</p>

<h4><a id="user-content-parameters-8" class="anchor" href="#parameters-8" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Parameters</h4>

<h6><a id="user-content-ensure-6" class="anchor" href="#ensure-6" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ensure</code></h6>

<p>Determine whether the neighbor config should be present or not. Valid values are 'present' and 'absent'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-asn-2" class="anchor" href="#asn-2" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>asn</code></h5>

<p>BGP autonomous system number. Required. Valid values are String, Integer in  ASPLAIN or ASDOT notation.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-vrf-2" class="anchor" href="#vrf-2" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>vrf</code></h5>

<p>VRF name. Required. Valid values are string. The name 'default' is a valid VRF representing the global bgp.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-neighbor" class="anchor" href="#neighbor" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>neighbor</code></h5>

<p>Neighbor Identifier. Required. Valid values are string. Neighbors may use IPv4 or IPv6 notation, with or without prefix length.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-description" class="anchor" href="#description" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>description</code></h5>

<p>Description of the neighbor. Valid value is string.</p>

<p>Specify source interface of BGP session and updates. Valid value is a string of the interface name.</p>

<h2></h2>

<h3><a id="user-content-type-cisco_bgp_neighbor_af" class="anchor" href="#type-cisco_bgp_neighbor_af" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Type: cisco_bgp_neighbor_af</h3>

<p>Manages configuration of a BGP Neighbor Address-family instance.</p>

<h4><a id="user-content-parameters-9" class="anchor" href="#parameters-9" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Parameters</h4>

<h6><a id="user-content-ensure-7" class="anchor" href="#ensure-7" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ensure</code></h6>

<p>Determine whether the neighbor address family config should be present or not.
Valid values are 'present' and 'absent'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-asn-3" class="anchor" href="#asn-3" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>asn</code></h5>

<p>BGP autonomous system number. Required. Valid values are String, Integer in ASPLAIN or
ASDOT notation.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-vrf-3" class="anchor" href="#vrf-3" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>vrf</code></h5>

<p>VRF name. Required. Valid values are string. The name 'default' is a valid VRF representing the global bgp.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-neighbor-1" class="anchor" href="#neighbor-1" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>neighbor</code></h5>

<p>Neighbor Identifier. Required. Valid values are string. Neighbors may use IPv4 or IPv6 notation, with or without a subnet mask.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-afi-2" class="anchor" href="#afi-2" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>afi</code></h5>

<p>Neighbor Address Family Identifier (AFI). Required. Valid values are string. Valid neighbor AFIs are <code>ipv4</code> and <code>ipv6</code>. Note that some AFI/SAFI address-families may not be supported with some neighbors; e.g. an ipv6 neighbor may not support an ipv4 multicast address-family.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-safi-1" class="anchor" href="#safi-1" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>safi</code></h5>

<p>Neighbor Sub Address Family Identifier (SAFI). Required. Valid values are string. Valid neighbor SAFIs are <code>unicast</code> and <code>multicast</code>. Note that some AFI/SAFI address-families may not be supported with some neighbors; e.g. an ipv6 neighbor may not support an ipv4 multicast address-family.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-advertise_map_exist" class="anchor" href="#advertise_map_exist" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>advertise_map_exist</code></h5>

<p>Conditional route advertisement. This property requires two route maps: an advertise-map and an exist-map. Valid values are an array specifying both the advertise-map name and the exist-map name, or simply 'default'; e.g. <code>['my_advertise_map', 'my_exist_map']</code>. This command is mutually exclusive with the advertise_map_non_exist property.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-advertise_map_non_exist" class="anchor" href="#advertise_map_non_exist" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>advertise_map_non_exist</code></h5>

<p>Conditional route advertisement. This property requires two route maps: an advertise-map and a non-exist-map. Valid values are an array specifying both the advertise-map name and the non-exist-map name, or simply 'default'; e.g. <code>['my_advertise_map', 'my_non_exist_map']</code>. This command is mutually exclusive with the advertise_map_exist property.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-allowas_in" class="anchor" href="#allowas_in" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>allowas_in</code></h5>

<p><code>allowas-in</code>. Valid values are true, false, or an integer value, which enables the command with a specific max-occurrences value. Related: <code>allowas_in_max</code>.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-allowas_in_max" class="anchor" href="#allowas_in_max" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>allowas_in_max</code></h5>

<p>Optional max-occurrences value for <code>allowas_in</code>. Valid values are an integer value or 'default'. Can be used independently or in conjunction with <code>allowas_in</code>.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-as_override" class="anchor" href="#as_override" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>as_override</code></h5>

<p><code>as-override</code>. Valid values are true, false, or 'default'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-additional_paths_receive-1" class="anchor" href="#additional_paths_receive-1" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>additional_paths_receive</code></h5>

<p><code>capability additional-paths receive</code>. Valid values are <code>enable</code> for basic command enablement; <code>disable</code> for disabling the command at the neighbor_af level (it adds the <code>disable</code> keyword to the basic command); and <code>inherit</code> to remove the command at this level (the command value is inherited from a higher BGP layer).</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-additional_paths_send-1" class="anchor" href="#additional_paths_send-1" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>additional_paths_send</code></h5>

<p><code>capability additional-paths send</code>. Valid values are <code>enable</code> for basic command enablement; <code>disable</code> for disabling the command at the neighbor_af level (it adds the <code>disable</code> keyword to the basic command); and <code>inherit</code> to remove the command at this level (the command value is inherited from a higher BGP layer).</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-default_originate" class="anchor" href="#default_originate" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>default_originate</code></h5>

<p><code>default-originate</code>. Valid values are True, False, or 'default'. Related: <code>default_originate_route_map</code>.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-default_originate_route_map" class="anchor" href="#default_originate_route_map" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>default_originate_route_map</code></h5>

<p>Optional route-map for the <code>default_originate</code> property. Can be used independently or in conjunction with <code>default_originate</code>. Valid values are a string defining a route-map name, or 'default'.</p>

<p><code>weight</code> value. Valid values are an integer value or 'default'.</p>

<h2></h2>

<h3><a id="user-content-type-cisco_interface" class="anchor" href="#type-cisco_interface" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Type: cisco_interface</h3>

<p>Manages a Cisco Network Interface. Any resource dependency should be run before the interface resource.</p>

<h4><a id="user-content-parameters-10" class="anchor" href="#parameters-10" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Parameters</h4>

<h5><a id="user-content-basic-interface-config-attributes" class="anchor" href="#basic-interface-config-attributes" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>Basic interface config attributes</h5>

<h6><a id="user-content-ensure-8" class="anchor" href="#ensure-8" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ensure</code></h6>

<p>Determine whether the interface config should be present or not. Valid values
are 'present' and 'absent'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-interface" class="anchor" href="#interface" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>interface</code></h6>

<p>Name of the interface on the network element. Valid value is a string.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-channel_group" class="anchor" href="#channel_group" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>channel_group</code></h6>

<p>channel_group is an aggregation of multiple physical interfaces that creates a logical interface. Valid values are 1 to 4096 and 'default'.</p>

<p>Note: On some platforms a normal side-effect of adding the channel-group property is that an independent port-channel interface will be created; however, removing the channel-group configuration by itself will not also remove the port-channel interface. Therefore, the port-channel interface itself may be explicitly removed by using the <code>cisco_interface</code> provider with <code>ensure =&gt; absent</code>.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-description-1" class="anchor" href="#description-1" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>description</code></h6>

<p>Description of the interface. Valid values are a string or the keyword 'default'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-duplex" class="anchor" href="#duplex" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>duplex</code></h6>

<p>Duplex of the interface. Valid values are 'full', and 'auto'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-speed" class="anchor" href="#speed" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>speed</code></h6>

<p>Speed of the interface. Valid values are 100, 1000, 10000, 40000, 1000000, and 'auto'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-shutdown-2" class="anchor" href="#shutdown-2" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>shutdown</code></h6>

<p>Shutdown state of the interface. Valid values are 'true', 'false', and
'default'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-switchport_mode" class="anchor" href="#switchport_mode" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>switchport_mode</code></h6>

<p>Switchport mode of the interface. To make an interface Layer 3, set
<code>switchport_mode</code> to 'disabled'. Valid values are 'disabled', 'access', 'tunnel', 'fex_fabric', 'trunk', and 'default'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-ipv4_acl_in" class="anchor" href="#ipv4_acl_in" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ipv4_acl_in</code></h6>

<p>Apply ipv4 access list on the interface in ingress direction. Access-list should be present on the network device 
prior this configuration. Valid values are string, keyword 'default'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-ipv4_acl_out" class="anchor" href="#ipv4_acl_out" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ipv4_acl_out</code></h6>

<p>Apply ipv4 access list on the interface in egress direction. Access-list should be present on the network device 
prior this configuration. Valid values are string, keyword 'default'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-ipv6_acl_in" class="anchor" href="#ipv6_acl_in" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ipv6_acl_in</code></h6>

prior this configuration. Valid values are string, keyword 'default'.</p>

<h6><a id="user-content-ipv6_acl_out" class="anchor" href="#ipv6_acl_out" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>ipv6_acl_out</code></h6>

<h5><a id="user-content-l2-interface-config-attributes" class="anchor" href="#l2-interface-config-attributes" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a>L2 interface config attributes</h5>

<h6><a id="user-content-access_vlan" class="anchor" href="#access_vlan" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>access_vlan</code></h6>

<p>The VLAN ID assigned to the interface. Valid values are an integer or the keyword
'default'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-encapsulation_dot1q" class="anchor" href="#encapsulation_dot1q" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>encapsulation_dot1q</code></h5>

<p>Enable IEEE 802.1Q encapsulation of traffic on a specified subinterface.
Valid values are integer, keyword 'default'.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-mtu" class="anchor" href="#mtu" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>mtu</code></h5>

<p>Maximum Trasnmission Unit size for frames received and sent on the specified
interface. Valid value is an integer.</p>

<h5><a id="user-content-community" class="anchor" href="#community" aria-hidden="true"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" role="img" version="1.1" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16"><path d="M4 9h1v1h-1c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5s1.55-3.5 3-3.5h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-0.91 2.72-2 3.25v-1.16c0.58-0.45 1-1.27 1-2.09 0-1.28-1.02-2.5-2-2.5H4c-0.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5s1 2.5 2 2.5z m9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5s-1.02 2.5-2 2.5H9c-0.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-0.83 0.42-1.64 1-2.09v-1.16c-1.09 0.53-2 1.84-2 3.25 0 1.81 1.55 3.5 3 3.5h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5s-1.5-3.5-3-3.5z"></path></svg></a><code>community</code></h5>
